* appears to be some sort of linked list task loop

828C: 34 01       PSHS  CC
828E: 0F 4E       CLR   $4E	* some variable
8290: 1A 50       ORCC  #$50	* disable interrupts
8292: 96 4E       LDA   $4E	* get variable
8294: 26 07       BNE   $829D	* zero? return
8296: 10 9E 59    LDY   $59	* some 16-bit variable
8299: 26 04       BNE   $829F	* zero? continue
829B: 0F 38       CLR   $38	* clear some variable
829D: 35 81       PULS  CC,PC ;(PUL? PC=RTS)

829F: EC A4       LDD   ,Y	* fetch value pointed to by Y
82A1: DD 59       STD   $59	* store value back
82A3: 26 02       BNE   $82A7	* zero?
82A5: DD 5B       STD   $5B	* no, store it here too
82A7: 1C AF       ANDCC #$AF	* enable interrupts
82A9: AD B8 02    JSR   [$02,Y]	* jump to next task in list?
82AC: 20 E2       BRA   $8290	* and loop

* calculate tuning from note number

* called with address of table in Y
* looks like if $80E3 is 0, we look at $80D1 for an offset
* otherwise if $80E3 is 2, zero it and continue
* or use $80E3 as the offset

AADC: 20 05       BRA   $AAE3	* branch to

*** loops around the filters setting resonance and cutoff to zero

zerofilter:
AE17: CE E4 18    LDU   #$E418		; DAC multiplexer, outputs off
AE1A: CC 00 00    LDD   #$0000
zerofilter2:
AE1D: BD F5 E7    JSR   setfilterdac
AE20: 11 83 E4 20 CMPU  #$E420		; done all filters?
AE24: 26 F7       BNE   zerofilter2	; no, continue
AE26: CE B0 52    LDU   #$B052		; in a block of data, variable storage?
AE29: CC 8A D7    LDD   #$8AD7		; possibly filter update routine
AE2C: 8E 8B BE    LDX   #$8BBE		; unmask IRQ and FIRQ
zerofilter3:
AE2F: ED C8 1C    STD   $1C,U		; store address of filter routine
AE32: AF C8 2B    STX   $2B,U		; store address of unmask routine
AE35: 6F C8 1A    CLR   $1A,U		; zero
AE38: 33 C8 4D    LEAU  $4D,U		; add 77 bytes
AE3B: 11 83 B2 BA CMPU  #$B2BA		; done all eight voices?
AE3F: 25 EE       BCS   zerofilter3	; no, loop
